 ) andhra pradesh main ekbar phir rajya ko 'vishesh shrenee' kaa darja die jane kii maang uthne lagi he

 andhra pradesh jis vishesh shrenee ke darje kii maang kar rahaa he, isamen shaamil rajyon ko centre kii taraf se kai phaayde milte hai
 What is special category state? The states included in the special category category are given more benefits and cooperation from the center than other states
 yah phayda va sahyog tex or anya yojanaon ke maamle main muhaiyaa kiya jaataa he
 On what basis are these statuses? There are certain standards set to include a state in the category of a particular state
 - pahari or durgam kshetra vaala rajya- kam jansankhya vaale rajyon ke saath hi yah un rajyon ko bhi miltaa he, jahaan adivasee janajatiyon kii acchhee-khaasi jansankhya he
 States close to international borders - States which are far behind in terms of financial and infrastructural development
 kya miltaa he phayda?vishesh shrenee ke rajyon ko centre kii taraf se vishesh sahyog praapt hota he
 These states are given more concession in central cooperation and tax than other states
 kendriya bajet main in rajyon ko hone vaale aavanton kaa kaaphi bada hissaa hota he
 At present, the 12th Financial Commission has explained the powers of special category states
 vishesh shrenee ke rajyon ko saamaanya kendriya sahyog main se 30 fisadi diya jaataa he
 While 70 percent of the cooperation is distributed among other states by looking at their population, per capita income and financial performance
 iske alaava vishesh shrenee ke rajyon ko exise or custom duties main bhi raahat di jaati he
 Centrally sponsored schemes (CCS) may also allocate more funds to them
 kya he andhra kaa tark :vishesh shrenee ke rajya kii maang ko lekar andhra pradesh kaa andolan aaj se nahin he
 It started since Telangana was separated from it
 iske alaava 2014 main tatkaaleen pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne kaha tha ki andhra pradesh ke uttaradhikari rajya ko 5 saal ke liye vishesh shrenee ke rajya kaa darja diya jayega

 inako mila he yah darjaspecial category states athwa vishesh shrenee rajya kaa darja sabase pehle 1969 main diya gaya tha

 us dauraan is shrenee main assam, nagaland or jammu-kashmir ko shaamil kiya gaya tha
 Later eight more states were also included in this category
 isamen uttarakhand, meghalaya, arunachal pradesh, himachal pradesh, manipur, sikkim, tripura or mizoram ko shaamil kiya gaya he
